<h3><p id="[01]Entity Definition Properties">Entity Definition Properties</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

These properties are part of the Entity Definition as a whole and go before the Component or Component Groups. Make sure to place them before any Components, Component Groups or Events sections or they will be ignored.</br><h3><p id="do_not_upgrade">do_not_upgrade</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Disables all current and future backwards compatibility for this entity. If new components or properties are added or changed to the vanilla version of this entity, they will not be applied.</br><a href="#Index">Back to top</a><br><br>

<h3><p id="format_version">format_version</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Specifies the version of the game this entity was made in. If the version is lower than the current version, any changes made to the entity in the vanilla version will be applied to it.</br><a href="#Index">Back to top</a><br><br>

<h4>Vanilla entities that use this</h4>
{
  "minecraft:entity": {
    "format_version": "1.2.0",    "do_not_upgrade": {},
    "component_groups": {...} ...}</br>
<br><br>

<h3><p id="[02]Attributes">Attributes</p></h3>

<h3><p id="minecraft:attack">minecraft:attack</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Defines an entity's melee attack and any additional effects on it.</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>damage</td>
<td>Range [a, b]</td>
<td></td>
<td>Range of the random amount of damage the melee attack deals</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>effect_duration</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>0.0</td>
<td>Duration in seconds of the status ailment applied to the damaged entity</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>effect_name</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>Name of the status ailment to apply to an entity attacked by this entity's melee attack</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
<a href="#Index">Back to top</a><br><br>

<h3><p id="minecraft:spell_effects">minecraft:spell_effects</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Defines what mob effects to add and remove to the entity when adding this component.</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>add_effects</td>
<td>List</td>
<td></td>
<td>List of effects to add to this entity after adding this component</br><table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>effect</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>Effect to add to this entity. Includes 'duration' in seconds, 'amplifier' level, 'ambient' if it is to be considered an ambient effect, and 'visible' if the effect should be visible</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>remove_effects</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>List of names of effects to be removed from this entity after adding this component</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
<a href="#Index">Back to top</a><br><br>

<h3><p id="minecraft:strength">minecraft:strength</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Defines the entity's strength to carry items.</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>max</td>
<td>Integer</td>
<td>5</td>
<td>The maximum strength of this entity</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>value</td>
<td>Integer</td>
<td>1</td>
<td>The initial value of the strength</br></td>
</tr>
</table>

<h3><p id="minecraft:ambient_sound_interval">minecraft:ambient_sound_interval</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>range</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>16.0</td>
<td>Maximum time is seconds to randomly add to the ambient sound delay time.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>value</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>8.0</td>
<td>Minimum time in seconds before the entity plays its ambient sound again</br></td>
</tr>
</table>

<h3><p id="[05]Components">Components</p></h3>

<br><br>

<h3><p id="minecraft:addrider">minecraft:addrider</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Adds a rider to the entity. Requires minecraft:rideable.</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>entity_type</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>The entity type that will be riding this entity</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
<a href="#Index">Back to top</a><br><br>

<h3><p id="minecraft:ageable">minecraft:ageable</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Adds a timer for the entity to grow up. It can be accelerated by giving the entity the items it likes as defined by feedItems.</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>duration</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>1200.0</td>
<td>Amount of time before the entity grows</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>feedItems</td>
<td>List</td>
<td></td>
<td>List of items that can be fed to the entity. Includes 'item' for the item name and 'growth' to define how much time it grows up by</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>grow_up</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>Event to run when this entity grows up</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
<a href="#Index">Back to top</a><br><br>

<h3><p id="minecraft:angry">minecraft:angry</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Defines the entity's 'angry' state using a timer.</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>broadcastAnger</td>
<td>Boolean</td>
<td>false</td>
<td>If true, other entities of the same entity definition within the broadcastRange will also become angry</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>broadcastRange</td>
<td>Integer</td>
<td>20</td>
<td>Distance in blocks within which other entities of the same entity definition will become angry</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>calm_event</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>Event to run after the number of seconds specified in duration expires (when the entity stops being 'angry')</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>duration</td>
<td>Integer</td>
<td>25</td>
<td>The amount of time in seconds that the entity will be angry</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>duration_delta</td>
<td>Integer</td>
<td>0</td>
<td>Variance in seconds added to the duration [-delta, delta]</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
<a href="#Index">Back to top</a><br><br>

<h3><p id="minecraft:boostable">minecraft:boostable</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Defines the conditions and behavior of a rideable entity's boost</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>boost_items</td>
<td>List</td>
<td></td>
<td>List of items that can be used to boost while riding this entity. Each item has the following properties:</br><table border="1">

<h3><p id="minecraft:rail_sensor">minecraft:rail_sensor</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Defines the behavior of the entity when the rail gets activated or deactivated.</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>check_block_types</td>
<td>Boolean</td>
<td>false</td>
<td>If true, on tick this entity will trigger its on_deactivate behavior</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>eject_on_activate</td>
<td>Boolean</td>
<td>true</td>
<td>If true, this entity will eject all of its riders when it passes over an activated rail</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>eject_on_deactivate</td>
<td>Boolean</td>
<td>false</td>
<td>If true, this entity will eject all of its riders when it passes over a deactivated rail</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>on_activate</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>Event to call when the rail is activated</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>on_deactivate</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>Event to call when the rail is deactivated</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>tick_command_block_on_activate</td>
<td>Boolean</td>

<h3><p id="minecraft:behavior.avoid_mob_type">minecraft:behavior.avoid_mob_type</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Allows this entity to avoid certain mob types.</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>entity_types</td>
<td>JSON Object</td>
<td></td>
<td>List of entity types this mob avoids.</br><table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>filters</td>
<td>Minecraft Filter</td>
<td></td>
<td>Conditions that make this entry in the list valid</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>max_dist</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>16</td>
<td>Maximum distance this mob can be away to be a valid choice</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>must_see</td>
<td>Boolean</td>
<td>false</td>
<td>If true, the mob has to be visible to be a valid choice</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>sprint_speed_multiplier</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>1.0</td>
<td>Multiplier for the running speed. A value of 1.0 means the speed is unchanged</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>

</table>
</td>

<tr>

<td>0.0</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td>max_flee</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>0.5</td>
<td>Distance in blocks within the mob considers it should stop fleeing.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>probability_per_strength</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>1.0</td>
<td>Determines how likely it is that this entity will stop avoiding another entity based on that entity's strength</br></td>

<tr>
<td>sprint_speed_multiplier</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>1.0</td>
<td>Multiplier for running speed. 1.0 means keep the regular speed, while higher numbers make the running speed faster</br></td>

<td>Time range to look at the entity</br></td>

<td>Decimal</td>
<td>0.02</td>
<td>The probability of looking at the target. A value of 1.00 is 100%</br></td>
</tr>
</table>

<td>0</td>
<td>Maximum amount of time in seconds the entity will wait after an attack before launching another</br></td>

<tr>
<td>attack_interval_min</td>

<tr>
<td>attack_radius</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>0.0</td>
<td>Maxmimum distance the target can be for this mob to fire. If the target is further away, this mob will move first before firing</br></td>

<td>1</td>

<td>0.0</td>
<td>The minimum amount of time in ticks the mob has to charge before firing a charged attack</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>charge_shoot_trigger</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>0.0</td>
<td>The minimum amount of time in ticks for the mob to start charging a charged shot. Must be greater than 0 to enable burst shots</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>speed_multiplier</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>1.0</td>
<td>Movement speed multiplier of the mob when using this AI Goal</br></td>
</tr>
</table>

<h4>Description</h4>

Allows the mob to attack the player by summoning other entities.</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>summon_choices</td>
<td>List</td>
<td></td>
<td>List of spells for the mob to use to summon entities. Each spell has the following parameters:</br><table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>cast_duration</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>Total delay of the steps</td>
<td>Time in seconds the spell casting will take</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>cooldown_time</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>0.0</td>
<td>Time in seconds the mob has to wait before using the spell again</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>do_casting</td>
<td>Boolean</td>
<td>true</td>
<td>If true, the mob will do the casting animations and render spell particles</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>filters</td>
<td>Minecraft Filter</td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>max_activation_range</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>-1.0</td>
<td>Upper bound of the activation distance in blocks for this spell</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>min_activation_range</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>1.0</td>
<td>Lower bound of the activation distance in blocks for this spell</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>particle_color</td>
<td>Integer</td>
<td>0</td>
<td>The color of the particles for this spell</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>sequence</td>
<td>List</td>
<td></td>
<td>List of steps for the spell. Each step has the following parameters:</br><table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>base_delay</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>0.0</td>
<td>Amount of time in seconds to wait before this step starts</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>delay_per_summon</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>0.0</td>
<td>Amount of time in seconds before each entity is summoned in this step</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>entity_lifespan</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>-1.0</td>
<td>Amount of time in seconds that the spawned entity will be alive for. A value of -1.0 means it will remain alive for as long as it can</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>entity_type</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>The entity type of the entities we will spawn in this step</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>num_entities_spawned</td>
<td>Integer</td>
<td>1</td>
<td>Number of entities that will be spawned in this step</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>shape</td>
<td>String</td>
<td>line</td>
<td>The base shape of this step. Valid values are circle and line</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>size</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>1.0</td>
<td>The base size of the entity</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>sound_event</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>The sound event to play for this step</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>summon_cap</td>
<td>Integer</td>
<td>0</td>
<td>Maximum number of summoned entities at any given time</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>summon_cap_radius</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>0.0</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>target</td>
<td>String</td>
<td>self</td>
<td>The target of the spell. This is where the spell will start (line will start here, circle will be centered here)</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>start_sound_event</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>The sound event to play when using this spell</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>weight</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td>0.0</td>
<td>The weight of this spell. Controls how likely the mob is to choose this spell when casting one</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<h3><p id="[07]Filters">Filters</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Filters allow data objects to specify test critera which allows their use.</br></br>: For example, a model that includes a filter will only be used when the filter criteria is true.</br></br></br></br>: A typical filter consists of four paramters:</br></br>: name: the name of the test to apply.</br></br>: domain: the domain the test should be performed in. An armor slot, for example. This parameter is only used by a few tests.</br></br>: operator: the comparison to apply with the value, such as 'equal' or 'greater'.</br></br>: value: the value being compared with the test.</br></br></br></br>: A typical filter looks like the following:</br></br>: { "test" : "moon_intensity", "subject" : "self", "operator" : "greater", "value" : "0.5" } </br></br>: Which results in the calling entity (self) calculating the moon_intensity at its location and returning true if the result is greater than 0.5.</br></br></br></br>: Tests can be combined into groups using the collections 'all_of' and 'any_of'.</br></br>: All tests in an 'all_of' group must pass in order for the group to pass.</br></br>: One or more tests in an 'any_of' group must pass in order for the group to pass.</br></br></br></br>: Example:</br></br>: "all_of" : [</br></br>:   { "test" : "moon_intensity", "subject" : "self", "operator" : "greater", "value" : "0.5" }, </br></br>:   { "test" : "in_water", "subject" : "target", "operator" : "equal", "value" : "true" } </br></br>: ]</br></br>: This filter group will pass only when the moon_intensity is greater than 0.5 AND the caller's target entity is standing in water.</br><h3><p id="clock_time">clock_time</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Compares the current time with a float value in the range (0.0, 1.0).
0.0= Noon
0.25= Sunset
0.5= Midnight
0.75= Sunrise</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>operator</td>
<td>String</td>
<td>equals</td>
<td>(Optional) The comparison to apply with 'value'.</br><table border="1">
<tr> <th>Options</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>!=</td>
<td>Test for inequality.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><</td>
<td>Test for less-than the value.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><=</td>
<td>Test for less-than or equal to the value.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><></td>
<td>Test for inequality.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>=</td>
<td>Test for equality.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>==</td>
<td>Test for equality.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>></td>
<td>Test for greater-than the value.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>>=</td>
<td>Test for greater-than or equal to the value.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>equals</td>
<td>Test for equality.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>not</td>
<td>Test for inequality.</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>subject</td>
<td>String</td>
<td>self</td>
<td>(Optional) The subject of this filter test.</br><table border="1">
<tr> <th>Options</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>other</td>
<td>The other member of an interaction, not the caller.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>parent</td>
<td>The caller's current parent.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>player</td>
<td>The player involved with the interaction.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>self</td>
<td>The entity or object calling the test</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>target</td>
<td>The caller's current target.</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>value</td>
<td>Decimal</td>
<td></td>
<td>(Required) A floating point value.</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
<h4>Examples</h4>
{ "test": "clock_time", "subject": "self", "operator": "equals", "value": "0.00" }</br>
{ "test": "clock_time", "value": "0.00" }</br>

<h3><p id="is_underground">is_underground</p></h3>

<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>event</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>The event to run when the conditions for this trigger are met</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>filters</td>
<td>Minecraft Filter</td>
<td></td>
<td>The list of conditions for this trigger</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>target</td>
<td>String</td>
<td>self</td>
<td>The target of the event</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
<a href="#Index">Back to top</a><br><br>

<h3><p id="minecraft:on_target_escape">minecraft:on_target_escape</p></h3>

<h4>Description</h4>

Adds a trigger to call when this entity loses the target it currently has.</br><h4>Parameters</h4>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Type</th> <th>Default Value</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>event</td>
<td>String</td>
<td></td>
<td>The event to run when the conditions for this trigger are met</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>filters</td>
<td>Minecraft Filter</td>
<td></td>
<td>The list of conditions for this trigger</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>target</td>
<td>String</td>
<td>self</td>
<td>The target of the event</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
<a href="#Index">Back to top</a><br><br>

<br><br>

<h3><p id="[09]Built-in Events">Built-in Events</p></h3>

<table border="1">
<tr> <th>Name</th> <th>Description</th> </tr>
<tr>
<td>minecraft:entity_born</td>
<td>Event called on an entity that is spawned through two entities breeding.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>minecraft:entity_spawned</td>
<td>Event called on an entity that is placed in the level.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>minecraft:entity_transformed</td>
<td>Event called on an entity that transforms into another entity.</br></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>minecraft:on_prime</td>
<td>Event called on an entity whose fuse is lit and is ready to explode.</br></td>
</tr>
</table>
